UNIVERSITY CALENDAR FOR THE UNDERGRADUATE SCHOOL 

FOR THE YEAR 1950-51 
First Semester 
Sept. 11, 12, 1 3 .........................................................................................Registration with the Director of (Mon., Tues., Wed.) Student Accounts and with the Deans for courses in the first 

sem ester. 

Sept. 14 (Thurs.)..............................................................................................Classes begin at 8:00 a.m . 
Sept. 17 (S un.).....................................................................................Formal opening of the schoolyear with Solemn Mass and sermon by the President. 
Sept. 18 (Mon. ) .....................................................................................Latest date for essential class changes. 
Oct. 13 (Fri.) .............................................................................. Founder's Day (no classes). 
Nov. 1 (Wed.) .....................................................................................All Saints Day (noclasses). 
Nov. 15 (W ed .).....................................................................................Midsemester reports of deficient students. 
Nov. 16 to 2 2 .....................................................................................Preregistration in courses for 

(Thurs. to Wed.) the second semester of1950-51. (See Academic Regulation 113, General Bulletin). 
Nov. 23 (Thurs.).....................................................................................Thanksgiving Day (no classes). 
Dec. 8 (Fri.) .....................................................................................Feast of the Immaculate Con­ception (no classes). 
Dec. 16 (Sat.) .-.........................................................................Latest date for comprehensive examinations, anddissertations of undergraduates. 
Dec. 20 (Wed.) .....................................................................................First day of Christmas vacation. 
Jan. 3 (Wed.) .....................................................................................Classes resumed at 8:00 a. m. 
Jan. 18 to 25................................................................................................Semester examinations in all (Thurs. to Thurs.) courses. 
Jan. 28 (S u n .).....................................................................................January Commencement Exer­cises.

a. m., Washington Hall. At­tendance required as part-fulfillment of the requirements for June Graduation.

RESIDENCE 





RESIDENCE HALL PHONES 
The purpose of the hall extension phones is for the reception of necessary long distance calls to students from family and friends. In order to keep trunklines open, the operators on the Notre Dame switchboard have been instructed not to put through any local calls on hall extension phones. Instruct your friends locally to call the pay phone number in your hall. Please answer the phones for students'use in your hall. You do your fellow student a service.

CODES AND ABBREVIATIONS 
Explanation of the code which follows the student's name in parentheses. 
The letter and number which follow each student's name in parentheses are to be indicated according to the following code. The letter desig­nates the college, and the number indicates the class; for example. 
Smith, John J., (E-l) indicates Engineering, freshman.
